           <dd>&#x2022; also pl.), brightness (of the sky) <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#RV">RV.</a> &amp;c.            <dd>&#x2022; or <em>&#x00fa;ttara</em>, i, 9, l </dd>

           <dd>&#x2022; also personifled as 'fire' on earth, 'ether or air' in the intermediate region, and 'sun' in the sky <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#&#x015a;Br">&#x015a;Br.</a> xi, 5, 8, 2 <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#S&#x0101;&#x1e45;kh&#x015a;r">S&#x0101;&#x1e45;kh&#x015a;r.</a> xvi, 21, 2, &amp;c </dd>
